<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уронить.html>урони́ть</a> (4276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-рони́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ronítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*roniti</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уронить.html>урони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uronítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ронять.html>роня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drop (something), usually unintentionally</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:урочище.html>уро́чище</a> (22521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уро́чить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uróčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ище</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-išče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:урочище.html>уро́чище</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uróčišče</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:урочище.html>уро́чища</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:урочище.html>уро́чища</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:урочище.html>уро́чищ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> natural boundary, natural border <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. a mountain chain or river</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> natural landmark <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. a copse of trees in an open plain</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***ус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>ус</a> (1778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">усъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ǫsъ</i> lt; <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vǫsъ</i> lt; <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vǫdsъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*wónsa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wondʰsom</i>, s-expansion of root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wendʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hair, wool, beard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>ус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">us</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>у́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>усы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>усо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> moustache</li>
<li>whisker</li>
<li>feeler, antenna</li>
<li>tendril, awn</li></ol>

***усадить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усадить.html>усади́ть</a> (5769)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадить.html>усади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усаживать.html>уса́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make or let someone sit down, to seat</li>
<li>to ask someone to sit down</li>
<li>to set (someone to do something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усадить.html>усади́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usadítʹ</b> kovó-libo za rabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set someone to work</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to plant (e.g. trees or flowers)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усадьба.html>уса́дьба</a> (4797)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадить.html>усади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадьба.html>уса́дьба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usádʹba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадьба.html>уса́дьбы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадьба.html>уса́дьбы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадьба.html>уса́деб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>farmstead</li>
<li>homestead</li>
<li>place</li>
<li>barton</li>
<li>steading</li>
<li>hall <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a manor house</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>messuage</li>
<li>toft</li></ol>

***усаживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усаживать.html>уса́живать</a> (17813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадить.html>усади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усаживать.html>уса́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usáživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усадить.html>усади́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make or let someone sit down, to seat</li>
<li>to ask someone to sit down</li>
<li>to set (someone to do something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усаживать.html>уса́живать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usáživatʹ</b> kovó-libo za rabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set someone to work</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to plant (e.g. trees or flowers)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усаживаться.html>уса́живаться</a> (7185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усаживать.html>уса́живать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usáživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; pairing with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усесться.html>усе́сться</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uséstʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> corresponds to pairing between <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усаживаться.html>уса́живаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usáživatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усесться.html>усе́сться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sit down (comfortably), to take a seat</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усаживать.html>уса́живать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usáživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усваивать.html>усва́ивать</a> (17738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усвоить.html>усво́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usvóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усваивать.html>усва́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usváivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усвоить.html>усво́ить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to master, to learn</li>
<li>to adopt (a habit, a custom)</li>
<li>to digest, to assimilate</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усвоить.html>усво́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usvóitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усваивать.html>усва́ивать</a></b>)

<ol><li>to master, to learn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:усвоить.html>усво́или</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:название.html>назва́ния</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My s mályx let <b>usvóili</b> éti nazvánija.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We since [our] earliest years have been extracting ownership of these [words'] meanings.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to adopt (a habit or custom)</li>
<li>to digest, to assimilate</li></ol>

***усердие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усердие.html>усе́рдие</a> (10052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усердие.html>усе́рдие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usérdije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усердие.html>усе́рдия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усердие.html>усе́рдия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усердие.html>усе́рдий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>eagerness, zeal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усердие.html>усе́рдие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разум.html>ра́зуму</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">usérdije ne po rázumu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">more zeal than sense</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>diligence, assiduity</li></ol>

***усердствовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усердствовать.html>усе́рдствовать</a> (29460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усердие.html>усе́рдие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usérdije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ствовать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усердствовать.html>усе́рдствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usérdstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be diligent <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional, in something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be excessively zealous or eager</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усечь.html>усе́чь</a> (20308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усечь.html>усе́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uséčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усека́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut off, to truncate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to understand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усечь.html>усёк</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>usjók</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">got it?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***усеять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усеять.html>усе́ять</a> (10517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">séjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усеять.html>усе́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uséjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усе́ивать</b>)
</p>

***усидеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усидеть.html>усиде́ть</a> (20983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sidétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усидеть.html>усиде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usidétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уси́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remain sitting <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">after being pushed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sit still <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">despite one's desires or intentions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold on <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to a position or job</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to remain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a position or job</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stay in place, to refrain from leaving</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sit at the table and eat or drink (something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fully or in large quantities</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
